\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n}\n\n// Word to digit mapping - comprehensive\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1', 'want': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'tu': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3', 'free': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4', 'ford': '4',\n  'five': '5', 'fife': '5', 'hive': '5',\n  'six': '6', 'sicks': '6', 'sex': '6', 'seis': '6',\n  'seven': '7', 'sevn': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'ait': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9', 'mine': '9', 'line': '9', 'dine': '9'\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  if (!text) return '';\n  \n  // First extract any raw digits\n  const rawDigits = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  \n  // Then convert words to digits\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^\\w\\s]/g, '').split(/\\s+/);\n  let wordDigits = '';\n  \n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\n      wordDigits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    } else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) {\n      wordDigits += word;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Return whichever has more digits\n  const result = wordDigits.length >= rawDigits.length ? wordDigits : rawDigits;\n  console.log('[extractDigits] Input:', text, '\u2192 Output:', result);\n  return result;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (digits: string): string => {\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${clean.slice(0, 3)}-${clean.slice(3, 6)}-${clean.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const map: Record<string, string> = {\n    '0': 'zero', '1': 'one', '2': 'two', '3': 'three', '4': 'four',\n    '5': 'five', '6': 'six', '7': 'seven', '8': 'eight', '9': 'nine'\n  };\n  return digits.replace(/\\D/g, '').split('').map(d => map[d] || d).join(' ');\n};\n\nexport const useVoice = (options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\n  const { onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true } = options;\n  \n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\n\n  const synthRef = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Initialize speech recognition - THE CRITICAL PART\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n\n    const recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\n\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[useVoice] \u2705 STARTED - Now \n      if (text) {\n        setTranscript(text);\n      }\n\n      // Only process final results\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        console.log('[useVoice] Processing final result:',     }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recRef.current = recognition;\n\n    // Auto-start if requested\n    if (autoStart) {\n recRef.current.start();\n            console.log('[useVoice] \u2705 Started');\n          } catch (e) {\n            console.error('[useVoice] Auto-start failed:', e);\n          }\n        }\n (!synthRef.current) return;\n    \n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\n\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\n    utterance.pitch v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) ||\n                  voices[0];\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n\n }, []);\n\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n    isActiveRef.current = false;\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    setIsListening(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const pause = handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] \ud83d\udd22 Received voice digits:', digits);\n    \n    const newOtp = [...otp];\n    let idx = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\n    if (idx === -1) idx = 0;\n\n    for (const digit of digits) {\n      if (idx < 6) {\n        newOtp[idx] = digit;\n        idx++;\n      }\n    }\n\n    setOtp(newOtp);\n\n    // Check if complete\n    if (newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\n      const code = newOtp.join('');\n      if (code === DEMO_CODE) {\n        speak(\"Code verified! Try 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [otp, onVerified, speak]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Registering voice digit handler');\n    onVoiceDigits(handleVoiceDigits);\n  }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\n\n  // Focus first input on mount\n  useEffect(() => {\n    inputRefs.current[0]?.focus();\n  }, []);\n\n  const handleChange = (index: number, value: string) => {\n    if (!/^\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\n\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\n    newOtp[index] = value.slice(-1);\n    setOtp(newOtp);\n\n    // Auto-tab to next\n    if (value && index < 5) {\n      inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\n    }\n\n    // Check if complete\n    if (newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\n      const code = newOtp.join('');\n      if (code === DEMO_CODE) {\n        speak(\"Code verified!\");\n        setTimeout(onVerified, 500);\n      } else {\n        speak(\"Invalid code. Try 1 2 3 4 5 6.\");\n        setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n        inputRefs.current[0]?.focus();\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {\n    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) {\n      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n        Enter Verification Code\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n        Sent to <strong style={{ color: '#fff' }}>{phone}</strong>\n      </p>\n      <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '24px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\n        Demo code: <strong>1 2 3 4 5 6</strong>\n      </p>\n\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\n          <input\n            key={idx}\n            ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el}\n            type=\"text\"\n            inputMode=\"numeric\"\n            maxLength={1}\n            value={digit}\n            onChange={(e) => handleChange(idx, e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(idx, e)}\n            style={{\n              width: '55px',\n              height: '65px',\n              fontSize: '1.8em',\n              textAlign: 'center',\n              borderRadius: '12px',\n              border: `2px solid ${digit ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.5)'}`,\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontWeight: 600\n            }}\n          />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n\n      <button\n        onClick={() => speak(\"Resending code...\")}\n        style={{\n          background: 'none',\n          border: 'none',\n          color: THEME.gold,\n digits\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^\\\\w\\\\s]/g, '').split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let wordDigits = '';\\n  \\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\\n      wordDigits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    } else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) {\\n      wordDigits += word;\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  // Return whichever has more digits\\n  const result = wordDigits.length string): string => {\\n  const clean = digits.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (clean.length <= 3) return clean;\\n  if (clean.length <= 6) return `${clean.slice(0,   </div>\\n\\n      <button\\n        onClick={() => speak(\\\"Resending code...\\\")}\\n        style={{\\n          background: 'none',\\n          border: 'none',\\n          color: THEME.gold,\\n WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  if (!text) return '';\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^\\w\\s]/g, '').split(/\\s+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\n  }\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const m: Record<string,string> = {'0':'zero','1':'one','2':'two','3':'three','4':'four','5':'five','6':'six','7':'seven','8':'eight','9':'nine'};\n  return d.replace(/\\D/g,'').split('').map(x=>m[x]||x).join(' ');\n};\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n}\n\nexport const useVoice = (options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\n  const { onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true } = options;\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\n\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\n  const onCommandRef = useRef(onCommand);\n  const onDigitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\n\n  useEffect(() => { onCommandRef.current = onCommand; }, [onCommand]);\n  useEffect(() => { onDigitsRef.current = onDigits; }, [onDigits]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) return;\n\n    const rec = new SR();\n    rec.continuous = true;\n    rec.interimResults = true;\n    rec.lang = 'en-US';\n\n    rec.onstart = () => setIsListening(true);\n    rec.onresult = (e: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\n      const result = e.results[e.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      if (text) setTranscript(text);\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\n        if (digits.length > 0) onDigitsRef.current?.(digits);\n        onCommandRef.current?.(text.toLowerCase());\n      }\n    };\n    rec.onerror = (e: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      if (e.error === 'not-allowed') { setIsListening(false); isActiveRef.current = false; }\n    };\n    rec.onend = () => {\n      if (isActiveRef.current) setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 100);\n      else setIsListening(false);\n    };\n\n    recRef.current = rec;\n    if (autoStart) {\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\n      setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 300);\n    }\n    return () => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { rec.stop(); } catch(e){} };\n  }, [autoStart]);\n\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    setDisplayText(text);\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    u.rate = 1.0; u.pitch = 1.0;\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) || voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) || voices[0];\n    if (voice) u.voice = voice;\n    u.onend = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\n    u.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\n  }, []);\n\n  const stop = useCallback(() => { synthRef.current?.cancel(); setIsSpeaking(false); }, []);\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => { isActiveRef.current = true; try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch(e){} }, []);\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch(e){} setIsListening(false); }, []);\n  const pause = useCallback(() => { setIsPaused(true); isActiveRef.current = false; try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch(e){} }, []);\n  const resume = useCallback(() => { setIsPaused(false); isActiveRef.current = true; try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch(e){} }, []);\n\n  return { isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, transcript, displayText, speak, stop, startListening, stopListening, pause, resume };\n};\n\nexport default useVoice;\nEOF\necho \"  \u2705 Done\"\n\n# Try 1 2 3 4 5 6.\"); setOtp(['','','','','','']); }\n    }\n  }, [otp, onVerified, speak]);\n\n  useEffect(() => { onVoiceDigits(handleVoiceDigits); }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\n  useEffect(() => { inputRefs.current[0]?.focus(); }, []);\n\n  const handleChange = (index: number, value: string) => {\n    if (!/^\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\n    const newOtp = [...otp]; newOtp[index] = value.slice(-1); setOtp(newOtp);\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\n    if (newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\n      const code = newOtp.join('');\n      if (code === '123456') { speak(\"Verified!\"); setTimeout(onVerified, 500); }\n      else { speak(\"Invalid.\"); setOtp(['','','','','','']); inputRefs.current[0]?.focus(); }\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => { if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus(); };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px' }}>Enter Verification Code</h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>Sent to <strong style={{ color: '#fff' }}>{phone}</strong></p>\n      <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '24px' }}>Demo code: <strong>1 2 3 4 5 6</strong></p>\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\n          <input key={idx} ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el} type=\"text\" inputMode=\"numeric\" maxLength={1} value={digit} onChange={(e) => handleChange(idx, e.target.value)} onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(idx, e)} style={{ width: '55px', height: '65px', fontSize: '1.8em', textAlign: 'center', borderRadius: '12px', border: `2px solid ${digit ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.5)'}`, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', color: '#fff', fontWeight: 600 }} />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n      <button onClick={() => speak(\"Resending...\")} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: THEME.gold, cursor: 'pointer', textDecoration: 'underline' }}>Resend Code</button>\n      <p style={{ color: '#555', marginTop: '24px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\ud83d\udca1 Say: \"one two three four five six\"</p>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VendorOTP;\nEOF\necho \"  \u2705 Done\"\n\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# STEP 7: VendorProfile.tsx\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\necho \"\"\necho \"[7/12] Creating VendorProfile.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorProfile.tsx\" << 'EOF'\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\n\ninterface Props { profile: string; 'react';\n\ninterface Props { fileName?: string; vendorId?: string; vendorName?: string; onComplete: (products: any[]) => void; speak: (text: string) => void; onBrowseHome?: () => void; }\n\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\n\nconst STEPS = [\n  { id: 1, label: 'Parsing catalog', icon: '\ud83d\udccb', duration: 2500, say: \"Step 1: Parsing your catalog structure.\" },\n  { id: 2, label: 'Extracting images', icon: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', duration: 3000, say: \"Step 2: Extracting product images.\" },\n  { id: 3, label: 'AI enhancement', icon: '\u2728', duration: 3500, onComplete, speak, onBrowseHome }) => {\n  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(0);\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\n  const [stats, setStats] = useState({ images: 0, tables: \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[3/12] Creating useVoice.ts...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/common/useVoice.ts\\\" << 'EOF'\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  if (!text) return '';\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^\\\\w\\\\s]/g, '').split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\\n  }\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const m: Record<string,string> = {'0':'zero','1':'one','2':'two','3':'three','4':'four','5':'five','6':'six','7':'seven','8':'eight','9':'nine'};\\n  return d.replace(/\\\\D/g,'').split('').map(x=>m[x]||x).join(' ');\\n};\\n\\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\nexport const useVoice = (options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) => {\\n  const { onCommand, onDigits, autoStart = true } = options;\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\\n\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\\n  const onCommandRef = useRef(onCommand);\\n  const onDigitsRef = useRef(onDigits);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => { onCommandRef.current = onCommand; }, [onCommand]);\\n  useEffect(() => { onDigitsRef.current = onDigits; }, [onDigits]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) return;\\n\\n    const rec = new SR();\\n    rec.continuous = true;\\n    rec.interimResults = true;\\n    rec.lang = 'en-US';\\n\\n    rec.onstart = () => setIsListening(true);\\n    rec.onresult = (e: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\\n      const result = e.results[e.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      if (text) setTranscript(text);\\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\\n        const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n        if (digits.length > 0) onDigitsRef.current?.(digits);\\n        onCommandRef.current?.(text.toLowerCase());\\n      }\\n    };\\n    rec.onerror = (e: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      if (e.error === 'not-allowed') { setIsListening(false); isActiveRef.current = false; }\\n    };\\n    rec.onend = () => {\\n      if (isActiveRef.current) setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 100);\\n      else setIsListening(false);\\n    };\\n\\n    recRef.current = rec;\\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      isActiveRef.current = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 300);\\n    }\\n    return () => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { rec.stop(); } catch(e){} };\\n  }, [autoStart]);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    setDisplayText(text);\\n    if (!synthRef.current) return;\\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    u.rate = 1.0; u.pitch = 1.0;\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) || voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) || voices[0];\\n    if (voice) u.voice = voice;\\n    u.onend = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    u.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const stop = useCallback(() => { synthRef.current?.cancel(); setIsSpeaking(false); }, []);\\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => { isActiveRef.current = true; try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch(e){} }, []);\\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch(e){} setIsListening(false); }, []);\\n  const pause = useCallback(() => { setIsPaused(true); isActiveRef.current = false; try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch(e){} }, []);\\n  const resume = useCallback(() => { setIsPaused(false); isActiveRef.current = true; try { recRef.current?.start(); } catch(e){} }, []);\\n\\n  return { isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, transcript, displayText, speak, stop, startListening, stopListening, pause, resume };\\n};\\n\\nexport default useVoice;\\nEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Done\\\"\\n\\n# onVerified: () => void; speak: (text: string) => void; onVoiceDigits: (handler: (digits: string) => void) => void; }\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorOTP: React.FC<Props> = ({ phone, onVerified, speak, onVoiceDigits }) => {\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\\n  const inputRefs = useRef<(HTMLInputElement | null)[]>([]);\\n\\n  const handleVoiceDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    const newOtp = [...otp];\\n    let idx = newOtp.findIndex(d => d === '');\\n    if (idx === -1) idx = 0;\\n    for (const digit of digits) { if (idx < 6) { newOtp[idx] = digit; idx++; } }\\n    setOtp(newOtp);\\n    if (newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\\n      const code = newOtp.join('');\\n      if (code === '123456') { speak(\\\"Verified!\\\"); setTimeout(onVerified, 500); }\\n      else { speak(\\\"Invalid. Try 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\"); setOtp(['','','','','','']); }\\n    }\\n  }, [otp, onVerified, speak]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => { onVoiceDigits(handleVoiceDigits); }, [handleVoiceDigits, onVoiceDigits]);\\n  useEffect(() => { inputRefs.current[0]?.focus(); }, []);\\n\\n  const handleChange = (index: number, value: string) => {\\n    if (!/^\\\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\\n    const newOtp = [...otp]; newOtp[index] = value.slice(-1); setOtp(newOtp);\\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\\n    if (newOtp.every(d => d !== '')) {\\n      const code = newOtp.join('');\\n      if (code === '123456') { speak(\\\"Verified!\\\"); setTimeout(onVerified, 500); }\\n      else { speak(\\\"Invalid.\\\"); setOtp(['','','','','','']); inputRefs.current[0]?.focus(); }\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => { if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !otp[index] && index > 0) inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus(); };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udd10</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px' }}>Enter Verification Code</h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>Sent to <strong style={{ color: '#fff' }}>{phone}</strong></p>\\n      <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginBottom: '24px' }}>Demo code: <strong>1 2 3 4 5 6</strong></p>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\\n          <input key={idx} ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el} type=\\\"text\\\" inputMode=\\\"numeric\\\" maxLength={1} value={digit} onChange={(e) => handleChange(idx, e.target.value)} onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(idx, e)} style={{ width: '55px', height: '65px', fontSize: '1.8em', textAlign: 'center', borderRadius: '12px', border: `2px solid ${digit ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.5)'}`, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', color: '#fff', fontWeight: 600 }} />\\n        ))}\\n      </div>\\n      <button onClick={() => speak(\\\"Resending...\\\")} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: THEME.gold, cursor: 'pointer', textDecoration: 'underline' }}>Resend Code</button>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#555', marginTop: '24px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\\ud83d\\udca1 Say: \\\"one two three four five six\\\"</p>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VendorOTP;\\nEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Done\\\"\\n\\n# \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# STEP 7: VendorProfile.tsx\\n# \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[7/12] Creating VendorProfile.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorProfile.tsx\\\" << 'EOF'\\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface Props { profile: string; ${THEME.gold}`, borderRadius: '12px', padding: '16px', marginBottom: '16px', textAlign: 'left' }}>\\n            <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, margin: '0 0 8px', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\\u2728     <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center' }}>\\n          <button onClick={beautifyProfile} style={{ padding: '14px 28px', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VendorProfile;\\nEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Done\\\"\\n\\n# \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[9/12] Creating VendorUpload.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorUpload.tsx\\\" << 'EOF'\\nimport React, { useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface Props { onFileSelected: (file: File) => void; speak: (text: string) => void; }\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorUpload: React.FC<Props> = ({ onFileSelected, speak }) => {\\n  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);\\n  const [selectedFile, setSelectedFile] = useState<File | null>(null);\\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n\\n  const processFile = (file: File) => {\\n    const valid = ['.pdf', '.xlsx', '.xls', '.csv'].some(ext => file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith(ext));\\n    if (!valid) { speak(\\\"Sorry, I only accept PDF, Excel, or CSV.\\\"); return; }\\n    setSelectedFile(file);\\n    speak(`Got ${file.name}. Click Process to start.`);\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleDrop = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => { e.preventDefault(); setIsDragging(false); const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0]; if (file) processFile(file); }, []);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udce4</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.gold, marginTop: '16px' }}>Upload Your Catalog</h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>PDF, Excel, or CSV</p>\\n      <input ref={fileInputRef} type=\\\"file\\\" accept=\\\".pdf,.xlsx,.xls,.csv\\\" onChange={(e) => e.target.files?.[0] && processFile(e.target.files[0])} style={{ display: 'none' }} />\\n      {!selectedFile ? (\\n        <div onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()} onDragOver={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); setIsDragging(true); }} onDragLeave={() => setIsDragging(false)} onDrop={handleDrop} style={{ border: `3px dashed ${isDragging ? THEME.gold : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.5)'}`, borderRadius: '20px', padding: '50px', cursor: 'pointer', background: isDragging ? 'rgba(184,134,11,0.1)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)', maxWidth: '450px', margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n          <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\\ud83d\\udcc1</span>\\n          <p style={{ color: THEME.goldLight, marginTop: '16px' }}>{isDragging ? 'Drop here!' : 'Click or drag & drop'}</p>\\n        </div>\\n      ) : (\\n        <div style={{ background: 'rgba(184,134,11,0.1)', border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}`, borderRadius: '16px', padding: '24px', maxWidth: '450px', margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '16px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '2.5em' }}>\\ud83d\\udcc4</span>\\n            <div style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: 'left' }}>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontWeight: 500 }}>{selectedFile.name}</p>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#888', margin: '4px 0 0', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>{(selectedFile.size / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB</p>\\n            </div>\\n            <button onClick={() => setSelectedFile(null)} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer' }}>\\u2715</button>\\n          </div>\\n          <button onClick={() => onFileSelected(selectedFile)} style={{ padding:  </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VendorUpload;\\nEOF\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 Done\\\"\\n\\n# \"\"\necho \"[3/6] Creating VoiceTeleprompter...\"\n\nmkdir -p \"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/shared\"\ncat > \"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/shared/VoiceTeleprompter.tsx\" << 'EOF'\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface Props { onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void; context?: string; initialMessage?: string; minimized?: boolean; }\n\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B', teal: '#004236' };\n\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9' };\n\nconst VoiceTeleprompter: React.FC<Props> = ({ onCommand, context = 'home', initialMessage = \"I'm Mr. V. How can I help?\", minimized: initialMinimized = false }) => {\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState(initialMessage);\n  const [isMinimized, setIsMinimized] = useState(initialMinimized);\n  const [mode, setMode] = useState<'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text'>('interactive');\n\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\n\n  useEffect(() => { if (typeof window !== 'undefined') synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis; }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) return;\n\n    const rec = new SR();\n    rec.continuous = true; rec.interimResults = true; rec.lang = 'en-US';\n    rec.onstart = () => setIsListening(true);\n    rec.onresult = (e: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\n      const result = e.results[e.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      if (text) setTranscript(text);\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\n        if (cmd.includes('stop')) { stopSpeaking(); return; }\n        onCommand?.(cmd);\n      }\n    };\n    rec.onerror = (e: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => { if (e.error === 'not-allowed') { setIsListening(false); isActiveRef.current = false; } };\n    rec.onend = () => { if (isActiveRef.current) setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 100); else setIsListening(false); };\n    \n    recRef.current = rec;\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\n    setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 500);\n    return () => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { rec.stop(); } catch(e){} };\n  }, []);\n\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    if (!synthRef.current || mode === 'text') return;\n    synthRef.current.cancel(); setDisplayText(text); setIsSpeaking(true);\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text); u.rate = 1.0;\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) || voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) || voices[0];\n    if (voice) u.voice = voice;\n    u.onend = () => setIsSpeaking(false); u.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\n  }, [mode]);\n\n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => { synthRef.current?.cancel(); setIsSpeaking(false); }, []);\n  const toggleListening = useCallback(() => { if (isActiveRef.current) { isActiveRef.current = false; if (c.includes('close') || c.includes('exit')) { voice.stop(); onClose(); return; }\\n    if (c.includes('back')) { goBack(); return; }\\n    if (c.includes('next')) { goNext(); return; }\\n    \\n \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"[3/6] Creating VoiceTeleprompter...\\\"\\n\\nmkdir -p \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/shared\\\"\\ncat > \\\"$WORKING_DIR/src/components/shared/VoiceTeleprompter.tsx\\\" << 'EOF'\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface Props { onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void; context?: string; initialMessage?: string; minimized?: boolean; }\\n\\nconst THEME = { gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B', teal: '#004236' };\\n\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9' };\\n\\nconst VoiceTeleprompter: React.FC<Props> = ({ onCommand, context = 'home', initialMessage = \\\"I'm Mr. V. How can I help?\\\", minimized: initialMinimized = false }) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState(initialMessage);\\n  const [isMinimized, setIsMinimized] = useState(initialMinimized);\\n  const [mode, setMode] = useState<'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text'>('interactive');\\n\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const recRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => { if (typeof window !== 'undefined') synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis; }, []);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) return;\\n\\n    const rec = new SR();\\n    rec.continuous = true; rec.interimResults = true; rec.lang = 'en-US';\\n    rec.onstart = () => setIsListening(true);\\n    rec.onresult = (e: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      if (!isActiveRef.current) return;\\n      const result = e.results[e.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      if (text) setTranscript(text);\\n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\\n        const cmd = text.toLowerCase();\\n        if (cmd.includes('stop')) { stopSpeaking(); return; }\\n        onCommand?.(cmd);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    rec.onerror = (e: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => { if (e.error === 'not-allowed') { setIsListening(false); isActiveRef.current = false; } };\\n    rec.onend = () => { if (isActiveRef.current) setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 100); else setIsListening(false); };\\n    \\n    recRef.current = rec;\\n    isActiveRef.current = true;\\n    setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch(e){} }, 500);\\n    return () => { isActiveRef.current = false; try { rec.stop(); } catch(e){} };\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    if (!synthRef.current || mode === 'text') return;\\n    synthRef.current.cancel(); setDisplayText(text); setIsSpeaking(true);\\n    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text); u.rate = 1.0;\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) || voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US')) || voices[0];\\n    if (voice) u.voice = voice;\\n    u.onend = () => setIsSpeaking(false); u.onerror = () => setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\\n  }, [mode]);\\n\\n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => { synthRef.current?.cancel(); setIsSpeaking(false); }, []);\\n  const toggleListening = useCallback(() => { if (isActiveRef.current) { isActiveRef.current = false;
